**Query**

## Access Guide

> Creator: Gong Mingming

> Updater: Chen Chuangxin

> Created Time: 2021-03-25 09:36:59

> Update Time: 2026-03-05 10:25:46

#### Name analysis:

**AppId: Generated by the system, bound to the corresponding store ID, used to determine the only application or the only store. ,Secret key: The encryption key generated by the ,system and used for authentication in communication. ,ApiUrl: Each store has its own specific calling url, which is used for the target address sent during communication. ,Push ​​address: Filled in by the caller of OpenApi. The system will call the specified interface to notify the caller of operations with notification behavior at runtime. **

#### Access steps

##### 1. Get the store backend

**Contact Baodian customer service to obtain the login account and password behind the store. **

##### 2. Obtain AppId and secret key

**Enter the store backend, settings, and open platform menu, and you can see the AppId and communication key corresponding to the interface. **

**[object Object]**

##### 4. Connect the interface and test it online

#### Notes:

**Push rules: The system will push the message after the operation is completed. If the push fails, it will be pushed again after 5 seconds, for a total of 5 times. If the push fails 5 times, the push will be stopped. ,Secret key management: The secret key is the only certificate for communicating with the system. Please keep it properly and do not disclose it. **

**Query**

## Signature rules

> Creator: Gong Mingming

> Updater: Gong Mingming

> Created Time: 2021-03-25 09:36:59

> Update Time: 2024-08-18 23:36:06

#### General parameters and business parameters

**Interface requests include "general parameters" and "business parameters": General parameters: parameters that each interface needs to use, including (appid, action, version, timestamp, sign)
Business parameters: parameters contained in the body. The parameters used by each business are different. **

#### Request data signature verification

**[object Object]**

**action: operation name, version: version number, timestamp: timestamp, sign: signature content, body: business subject data**

**Signature verification method: The generation rule of the signature (sign) is: appid + action + version + timestamp + body + key. After adding the above fields, the generated string is MD5 encrypted (uppercase). In the above example, the signature verification rule is: be559b49662c4b609c5944eda383fefdmember_join10.11.817238229675851234567890. MD5 encrypt this string and compare the result with the sign. **

#### Push data signature verification

**The response data is JSON containing two parameters:**

**[object Object]**

**timestamp: timestamp, sign: signature content, data: data content**

**Signature verification method: MD5 encrypt the appid+timestamp+data+key data, and compare the result with the sign. **

	"sign": "6e5d8fba6a3086550498a61e5a01baf3",
	"body": "{\"uid\": \"b5ba39a1-5bea-11ef-a734-0c42a1b7b4ae\",\"tradeNo\": \"7882967938834104325\",\"category\": 1001,\"storedCategory\": 1,\"storedValue\": 50,\"effectiveDays\": 0,\"bizCode\": \"7882967938834104327\",\"remark\": \"Purchase a package and receive 50 game coins\"}"

| body.storedValue | 50 | integer | Yes | Amount of stored value recorded |
| body.effectiveDays | 0 | integer | Yes | The number of days the stored value is valid in the account. If it is 0, it means it will not expire |

	"timestamp": "1723822967585",

    "id": "916908cb-4810-4797-bbcc-ff986b6a3fbc", // 【Primary key] Unique identification ID of the card template
    "chainId": 2,          // Belonging total assembly line/chain headquarters ID
    "shopId": 13256,       // The ID of the specific store that belongs to it
    "sourceName": "store",  // Coupon source description
    "employeeName": "Employee name",  // The name of the employee who originally created this template
    "lastOperator": "Employee name",  // The name of the operator who last modified the configuration

    // ====== 【Voucher categories and core attribute layers]======
    "category": 5,                     // 【Large category enumeration] 5 representatives“Stored Value Voucher”mechanism
    "categoryName": "Stored Value Voucher",      // Category name
    "couponName": "Automatically cancel marble coupons",    // Coupon name (the name displayed to front-end users and management terminals)
    "remark": "",                      // Coupon background text remarks
    "isEnabled": true,                 // 【Switch】Whether this coupon template is available, false means it will be stopped/removed.
    "useRangeType": 1,                 // 【Applicable store range] Usually 1 representative“Available nationwide/all chain stores”，Others may mean that they are only used in designated store groups.

    // ====== 【Life cycle validity control layer]======
    "effectiveMode": 1,                // 【Validity mode] 1 Usually code relative mode (that is, it is valid for X days after receiving the coupon, rather than a specific day, month, and year)
    "effectiveModeName": "Effective immediately",   // Corresponding to the Chinese meaning of the above enumeration
    "delayDays": 0,                    // Delayed effective days (0 means the coupon can be used immediately after receiving it)
    "days": 1,                         // Number of days of validity (combined with 0 above, it means: it will take effect immediately after receiving it, and the validity period is 1 day)
    "startTime": "2026-03-24 15:04:22.226", // If absolute date mode is used, this identifies the starting time point of the activity.
